Hitler Calls Meeting to Discuss the Locarno Treaty Considers Reply to Suggestions from Britain and France German Government Personnel Say Situation Deteriorating 26

London: The agreement established by the Locarno Conference is now awaiting a reply from the German government. The country's chief representative, Ribbentrop, will take a plane today to return to Berlin to seek instructions from Führer Hitler. (Havas dispatch on the 21st)

London: Germany's reply to the plan for a new Locarno Pact drawn up by Britain, France, Italy, and Belgium may not be issued tomorrow. The League of Nations is deeply convinced that this plan keeps the door to negotiations open. Hitler's special envoy, Ribbentrop, has returned to Berlin by plane to consult with Hitler. Hitler has also returned to Berlin from Hamburg to hold a meeting with government officials to discuss the matter. British Foreign Secretary Eden told Ribbentrop this morning that he could contact him at any time this week if there were matters to discuss. The British House of Commons is scheduled to hold a debate next Tuesday and will pay attention to the Rhineland issue. (Reuters dispatch on the 21st)

London: German Chief Representative Ribbentrop told British Foreign Secretary Eden today that Germany cannot accept any proposals for resolving the Rhineland issue if it cannot enjoy equal treatment. Eden replied that Germany and France should make mutual concessions to ease the current situation in order to resolve the issue of European security. (National News Agency dispatch on the 20th)

Berlin: According to a senior official of the German government last night, after closer review of the memorandum from Britain, France, Belgium, and Italy regarding the Locarno Pact, the overall situation has deteriorated since noon. The wording of the document tries its best to protect the Treaty of Versailles and is definitely not a bridge to a peaceful solution. The first impression of Berlin upon receiving news of the proposals from London was far from pleasant. The establishment of a demilitarized zone on the German border is not in line with the principle of mutual equality. The German public cannot understand the meaning of foreign troops stationed on German soil. As for the international conference, in addition to considering the proposals put forward by Hitler, a large number of other plans and proposals must also be resolved, which will be cumbersome and will inevitably waste time and achieve nothing. (Reuters dispatch on the 21st)

Hamburg: Hitler delivered an election speech here today to 50,000 people, saying, "I am now fighting against the oppression of other countries to fight for equality. I hope the people will support me. Other countries will henceforth treat us unfairly. The world should know that we will not retreat in the slightest from the demands for equality we have made. Those politicians who think that they can win Germany's cooperation by adding new slander to Germany, I pity their foolishness." This decision speech was very short and did not mention a word about the British White Paper. (Reuters dispatch on the 20th)

Hitler's Speech Not Satisfied with Amending Articles Berlin Newspapers Attack New Agreement 27

Hamburg: The news that Führer Hitler would come here to give a speech suddenly spread here this morning, and the atmosphere in the city suddenly became active. All sectors were busy preparing for the welcome. At noon, Mr. Hee arrived and the people cheered as if they were there. Mr. Hee then went to the lecture hall to deliver his speech on international events. Mr. Hee first recalled the hard work of the government in the past three years, and then asked the people to pay attention to the importance of this decision election. Later, he said that Germany's actions have attracted the attention of world public opinion. During this period, the government urgently needs the unanimous support of the people of the country as a backing. For this reason, he now wants to apply for a national referendum. Although he is pleased with all the achievements of the government, he still hopes that the people can help him fight externally so that other countries will no longer dare to despise Germany. Germany is not satisfied with amending the text of the articles. It deeply hopes that the hearts of the people of all countries who have despised and feared Germany for the past seventeen years since the war can seek a thorough reform. Germany has now put forward its peace plan to all countries in the world. If all countries still try to bind the German people with articles, it is naturally unacceptable, and how can all countries only blame Germany for forgetting their own obligations to the articles? (National News Agency dispatch on the 20th)

Hamburg: Führer Hitler delivered a speech here today to 40,000 members of the National Socialist Party, saying that if the Rhineland issue cannot be resolved fairly, Germany will go its own way. If other countries have not yet abandoned the spirit of the Treaty of Versailles, which has been spurned by Germany, Germany would rather be isolated. The current problem cannot be solved by amending the treaty. We should correct our thinking and no longer discriminate against Germany. Regarding the attitude of European countries, Mr. Hee said, "What is regrettable now is that politicians in other countries always have two mistakes: 1. Germany is now under the control of a dictator, 2. Germany can be treated arbitrarily. I want to cooperate, but they have succeeded in creating a new way to insult Germany through this cooperation. If they have foresight, this plan will inevitably be poisonous in the future." (National News Agency dispatch on the 20th)

Berlin: The German newspapers this morning commented on the Locarno plan agreed upon by Britain, France, Belgium, and Italy, and unanimously criticized it, saying that its proposal is a collective reckless gesture and that Germany will never accept it. It also said that it proves that the four countries have no sense of awareness and are trying to make the cursed era of Versailles reappear today. This kind of proposal, in a word, is absurd. (Reuters dispatch on the 21st)

Statement by British Foreign Secretary Britain's Goal is to Restore International Law Germany Must Show Sincerity if it Truly Desires Peace 28

London: British Foreign Secretary Eden spoke in the House of Commons today, reporting on the methods by which Britain, the United States, France, Italy, and Belgium resolved the situation caused by Germany's entry into the Rhineland. All the seats were full, and there were no empty seats in the visitors' gallery.

Eden said that the German government has repeatedly stated its desire to ease the tense situation, but it remains to be seen what contribution it is willing to make. The British government's main purpose is to restore the world's trust in international law and create a situation in which we can work together to rebuild a solid Europe. However, trust has been destroyed and is not easy to restore. The Foreign Secretary then briefly described the temporary measures to ensure that negotiations proceed and achieve a satisfactory outcome, so as to re-establish a European security system. In addition to agreeing to send some troops to participate in the international force stationed in the narrow area east of the border between Germany and France and between Germany and Belgium, the British government also agreed to re-declare the obligations of the Locarno Pact with other countries to help restore trust. At the same time, it also asked Germany to make a contribution, but in the situation created by Germany's entry into the Rhineland, he is convinced that all members of the House will feel that it is extremely reasonable to ask Germany to make a contribution. Judging from the moderate attitude expressed by the French and Belgian governments, France and Belgium have already made a sufficient contribution, so it cannot be said that it is unreasonable to ask Germany to make a contribution.

The Foreign Secretary then spoke about the proposed negotiations, saying that what is currently proposed is that the five signatory countries to the Locarno Pact must conduct negotiations based on the following:

1. Several proposals in Germany's memorandum of March 7.

2. The change in the current situation in the Rhineland.

3. Drafting of a mutual assistance treaty that all signatory countries to the Locarno Pact can join.

The second stage will be a world conference initiated by the League of Nations to consider the proposals put forward by Germany regarding: 1. Security, 2. Arms Limitation, 3. Economic Relations between Countries. However, although all parties are extremely unwilling for the negotiations to fail, we must prevent the possibility of failure. He will publish a White Paper after his speech, which contains the drafts of letters from the British and Italian governments to the French and Belgian governments. The House of Commons will know what the position of Britain and Italy will be after the negotiations fail. As far as the British government is concerned, we are prepared to accept this proposal. We sincerely hope that the German government will also accept it. The German government has repeatedly stated that it is willing to ease the situation. Now is the time for the German government to show how it will contribute to achieving this goal.

The White Paper mentioned by British Foreign Secretary Eden contains the following guarantees that the British and Italian governments will give to France and Belgium in the event that efforts to resolve the situation fail:

1. Consult on the new situation.

2. Provide assistance in accordance with any measures jointly agreed upon in accordance with the Locarno Treaty.

3. Adopt measures for mutual security to defend against unprovoked aggression.

4. Establish or continue contacts between the general staff of various countries.

5. Cooperate with the Executive Yuan of the League of Nations to seek the formulation of various beneficial proposals to maintain peace and respect international conventions. It is heard that the troops planned under the unarmed area police program by British responsible parties are just symbolic troops. (Reuters dispatch on the 20th)

Declaration of French Foreign Minister The Foundation of Peace Has Been Consolidated France Advocates But Has Not Fully Achieved 29

Paris: The Chamber of Deputies convened at 3:00 PM. Foreign Minister Flandin delivered a lengthy speech on the draft agreement established by the Locarno Conference. All members of the Chamber were silent and listened to the speech. The scene was extremely solemn. Flandin said, "In the past ten days or so, people have been panicked, all of them shaking their heads and frowning. Fortunately, the foundation of peace has been consolidated. What I contribute to you is this." The French government originally advocated that negotiations with Germany could only be held after the international system had fully returned to normal. However, during the London Conference, the French proposal was also not met with setbacks. The draft agreement stipulates that negotiations can only begin after all the conditions in it have been fully accepted by Germany, so as to formulate a new system for the Rhineland region and consider the peace plan put forward by German Führer Hitler. Flandin then pointed out that Britain, France, Belgium, and Italy have all agreed to reaffirm the obligations contained in the Locarno Treaty and that the general staff of Britain, France, and Belgium will conclude a military agreement to discuss mutual guarantee methods to supplement it. "Even if a general mutual assistance treaty is established to replace the Locarno Treaty, the above-mentioned mutual guarantee methods should still be included in the new treaty. This is clearly stipulated in the draft agreement of the Locarno Conference. The British government has now decided to faithfully abide by the obligations of the Locarno Treaty. Once a crisis occurs, it will fulfill its obligations unyieldingly to ensure France's security. As for the practical methods of guarantee, Britain has also agreed to discuss them with France at any time. I have obtained written guarantees from British Foreign Secretary Eden, the importance of which is understood by anyone in France. As far as France is concerned, Britain's participation in the ancestral guarantee method is an important stage in the relationship between Britain and France after the European War. Since the views and actions of the two countries are unified, their effectiveness in eliminating war is more significant than in 1914." Flandin then described the invitation to Germany to participate in the negotiations, saying that the results obtained by the signatory countries to the Locarno Pact at the London Conference are only the first stage. If Germany accepts the negotiations, there will be new hope for the future of European peace. The agreement drafted by the Locarno Conference is a whole. If Germany refuses to accept it, the governments of Britain, France, Belgium, and Italy will jointly implement the necessary measures. However, the expressions made by Germany are serious in nature and do not comply with the regulations. On the contrary, the demands we have made are mild in nature and their purpose is to test whether Führer Hitler is truly sincere. If the German government can understand this and accept our demands, so that our test can be successful, then we will look forward to it. Foreign Minister Flandin then pointed out that the collective security system must be extended to Central and Eastern Europe, and that if a strong peace is to be organized, both limiting armaments and easing economic tensions are essential. "We must now take the London Agreement as a starting point and work hard to build. This is incumbent on France, and it will definitely seek success with all sincerity. I sincerely hope that in the next few months, the dawn of peace will appear on the European sky and create a new era. However, we must still strive to become stronger, because at this moment there are still various possibilities, the nature of which is rather dim, so that European peace is still threatened. No matter what value the friendship we have concluded with other countries has, the urgent task at present is to rely on our own strength," he said. (Havas dispatch on the 20th)

Observation of Belgian Prime Minister If Germany Accepts the Proposal, War Can Be Avoided, Otherwise Internal Division Will Be Seen in Germany 30

Beiping: Belgian Prime Minister Tiran declared in the House of Representatives today that if Germany accepts the London proposal, the danger of war can be eliminated. He believes that if Germany refuses, there is a risk of internal disagreement within the country. (Reuters dispatch on the 20th) Belgian Prime Minister Tiran returned from London and attended the House of Representatives to report on the London negotiations and explained the draft agreement established by the Locarno Conference, saying that the international rule of law system has been respected. If Germany accepts the London Agreement, there is hope for the future of European peace. All members of the House cheered and paid tribute to the Prime Minister. German Department Firmly Rejects Observation of Londoners 32

League of Nations to Meet Tomorrow

London: Responsible personnel here recently declared that if the German government clearly refuses to consider the agreement established by the Locarno Conference, other countries will immediately implement it. Fortunately, the German government will not clearly refuse, but will put forward a counter-proposal, which other countries will also discuss. Even if Germany refuses to submit the mutual assistance treaty between France and Russia to the Permanent Court of International Justice in The Hague for adjudication, other countries will not use this as an excuse to suspend negotiations, because the current negotiations have entered the third stage (the first stage is the Executive Yuan of the League of Nations condemning Germany's violation of the treaty, the second stage is the follow-up measures to the violation of the treaty, and the third stage is the negotiations on the overall situation in Europe). Its goal is to consider the mutual assistance treaty in Eastern Europe, the sky treaty in Western Europe, and the non-aggression pact in Central Europe in accordance with the London Declaration issued by the Central French government on February 3 last year, and to convene an international conference within two months to study the new Locarno Treaty and other issues, including the issue of arms limitation. (Havas dispatch on the 21st)

London: British newspapers have expressed a hope that if Germany cannot accept the proposals for a new Locarno Treaty put forward by the four countries, it should at least put forward an answer and not completely refuse. If it is felt that Germany's opposition to the unilateral demilitarized zone is an obstacle to international reconciliation, the French government may cooperate to find other solutions. It seems that it may be possible to establish another bilateral zone and have the Allied forces of Britain and Italy stationed within the French border on the French-German border. The measures to be taken by the Executive Yuan in accordance with the second part of the draft agreement should be studied by a committee. 4. The other measures contained in the draft agreement that are only related to the signatory countries to the Locarno Pact will be filed. However, the above agenda is not immutable, because Germany should submit a reply to the draft agreement before next Monday, or it may overturn this agenda. Informed sources believe that Germany will demand revisions to several points in the draft agreement. For example, objections will be raised to seeking direct access to the Permanent Court of The Hague and establishing a temporary demilitarized zone on the east bank of the Rhine, the second of which, in Germany's view, is discriminatory and unacceptable to the country. German Election To Whom Does One "Campaign" 34

The tickets they cast are not allowed to be contrary to the list of candidates proposed by the government, but those who wish to abstain are allowed to do so. This election ticket is similar to the one used when the proportional table was adopted in the past. The only difference is that in the past there were more than 20 parties, but now there is only one party. There is a circle printed at the bottom of the election ticket. Voters only need to draw a cross in the circle to indicate the person they want to elect. Those who do not draw a cross will be regarded as invalid votes. (Havas dispatch on the 21st)

American Flood: Losses of 500 Million Yuan 35

More Than Two Hundred Dead

New York - The losses from the American floods are now estimated to be no less than 500 million yuan. There are concerns about food shortages and the spread of disease in the disaster areas. In western Pennsylvania alone, the losses amount to 100 million yuan. The situation in the disaster areas is extremely dire. Tens of thousands of people are saddened by the destruction of their assets. Washington, D.C. appears to have escaped danger as the water level of the Potomac River has receded slightly, but preventative measures have not been relaxed. The White House is surrounded by sandbags, an unusual sight. (Reuters, 21st)

New York - The floods in fourteen eastern states have claimed the lives of over two hundred and forty people to date. River levels continue to rise in Connecticut, New Hampshire, Maine, and Massachusetts. Martial law has been declared in Portland, Maine. In Pittsburgh, women and children broke into shops and looted them. Even moldy and rotten food was consumed with relish. Two hundred members of the Pennsylvania National Guard were deployed to maintain order, resulting in twelve injuries and multiple arrests. (Havas, 20th)

Anglo-American-French Conference Concludes After Four Months; Three-Nation Naval Treaty to Be Signed in London on the 25th; Treaty Details to Be Released Tomorrow 36

London - After four months of meetings, the naval conference has reached an agreement on a three-nation naval treaty to replace the expiring Washington Naval Treaty. The treaty will be signed at a plenary session at St. James's Palace on the 25th. The current participants are Britain, America, and France. Italy and Japan will be allowed to join at a later date. The treaty contains safeguard clauses that allow it to become invalid under certain circumstances. The safeguard clauses provide for the replacement of lost ships and the suspension of the treaty's effect during wartime, but it will remain in effect once hostilities cease. This decision was made at the final meeting, which lasted all night and ended at 1 p.m. today, with only a few hours of rest this morning. (Reuters, 21st)

London - The General Committee of the Naval Conference held a meeting this morning to review the draft naval treaty. Afterward, a statement was released stating, "The naval treaty is scheduled to be signed at 4 p.m. on March 26th in the Queen Anne Room of St. James's Palace. Representatives from the United States, France, Great Britain, and its self-governing dominions will sign the treaty at that time. Among the self-governing dominions of Great Britain, only the representative of the Irish Free State has expressed unwillingness to sign, citing respect for the freedom of the nation." At today's meeting, the General Committee reviewed and approved the following: The Italian delegation's general reservations regarding the tonnage of capital ships and the "non-construction zone" (meaning no ships may be built between the maximum tonnage of cruisers and the minimum tonnage of capital ships); The draft naval treaty, the original text, and the appended protocols. The representative of the Union of South Africa, a self-governing dominion of Great Britain, raised two reservations regarding the form adopted by the treaty and various conference documents. It was requested that these reservations be communicated to the Secretary-General of the League of Nations, Avenol, after signing, so that he could forward them to the governments of all member states of the League of Nations for consideration. (Havas, 21st)

London - The Anglo-French-American naval agreement will be released next Monday, and its contents are divided into three parts:

The first part stipulates that signatory countries should exchange shipbuilding programs and notify each other of all information before making any decisions to start shipbuilding. There are two methods: Signatory countries should notify each other of their annual shipbuilding programs within the first four months of each year. Each decision to build a ship should include notification to the other signatory countries of the new warship's tonnage, speed, caliber of guns, and number of personnel. In the case of aircraft carriers, the number of aircraft carried should also be included.

The second part stipulates various qualitative limitations and contains eight articles: The maximum tonnage of capital ships should be 35,000 tons, and the maximum caliber of guns should be 14 inches. However, this is conditional on the other two signatory countries of the Washington Naval Treaty (i.e., Japan and Italy) joining the agreement before January 1, 1937. Otherwise, the maximum caliber of guns will remain at 16 inches. The tonnage issue of capital ships should be renegotiated starting in 1940, with the hope of further reductions. The tonnage of Class B cruisers should be limited to 8,000 tons, and the caliber of guns should be limited to 6.1 inches (155mm). Signatory countries may retain their existing 10,000-ton cruisers, but may not build any more of these cruisers during the term of the naval treaty. Regarding the "non-construction zone," the construction of cruisers between 8,000 and 17,500 tons is prohibited. Guns below 10 inches are not allowed to be equipped on capital ships. The tonnage of submarines should be limited to 2,000 tons, and the caliber of guns should be limited to 4.7 inches (120mm). The tonnage of aircraft carriers should be limited to 23,000 tons, and the caliber of guns should be limited to 6.1 inches (155mm).

Tianjin - The diplomatic impasse between Hebei and Chahar has lasted for over ten days. Major General Sonosuke Matsumuro is expected to arrive in Tianjin on the 28th to meet with Tada and Nagami before proceeding to Peiping. Our side will continue negotiations after his arrival in Peiping. Xiao Zhenying is scheduled to return to Tianjin on the 23rd and will continue to work behind the scenes on this matter. (Special Dispatch, 21st)

Death of Soviet Physiologist Ivan Pavlov 39

(TASS, Leningrad, February 27th) The great physiologist Ivan Pavlov passed away at 2:52 a.m. on February 27th, at the age of 86 and a half. Pavlov was born in 1849. At the age of 25, he published his first work, for which he received a gold medal from the University of St. Petersburg. Pavlov and his students' research has been recognized worldwide. In 1904, he received the Nobel Prize and 50 scientific honors from countries around the world. He was revered as the mentor of physiologists worldwide. All of Pavlov's scientific work was based on strict materialism. For the last 35 years, he devoted himself to the study of neurophysiology and pathology. He regarded the highest nervous activity and mental activity as one, and studied mental phenomena with materialism. He recently asserted, "An important stage in human thought is about to dawn. At that time, physiology and psychology, objective and subjective, will be unified. At that time, the contradictions and opposition between perception and the body will be resolved or naturally eliminated." Scientists from all over the world listened to Pavlov's speeches at previous international neurological and physiological conferences. They will never forget Pavlov's words and demeanor at the International Physiological Conference held in the Soviet Union last year. Pavlov's work expanded after the Russian Revolution because the Soviet government provided him with particularly favorable conditions for his scientific work, providing all necessary materials and money. Moreover, with the expansion of the Leningrad laboratory, a small town was built near Leningrad specifically for his scientific work. Until recently, his mind was still full of courage, hope, and optimistic plans. In September 1934, on his 85th birthday, this venerable scientist, admired by all, was praised by the Soviet government, various Soviet public organizations, and scientists from around the world. He still insisted that he did not believe he was old, and that he still wanted and was able to work. Six days ago, he formulated his work plan for 1936, still with this determination. Unfortunately, death robbed him of his precious life. Pavlov's school has produced many talented Soviet physiologists and published a large number of works in the Soviet Union. It will certainly continue to complete the great work of Pavlov's lifelong efforts.

Public Enterprise Budget Standard Approved 59

Nanjing - The Finance Committee of the Central Political Council believes that the regulations governing public enterprise accounting systems are inadequate. However, the implementation of new regulations will take time, and there must be corresponding standards for compiling, reviewing, implementing, and supervising operating budgets. Therefore, six articles of the Provisional Standards for Public Enterprise Budgets were drafted and approved by the Central Political Council, and the National Government has issued an order to the Directorate-General of Budgets, Accounts and Statistics to submit the budget items of operating agencies to the government for review. Review Opinions on the Inheritance Tax Proposal 61

Nanjing - The proposal to implement the inheritance tax has been reviewed by the Executive Yuan, which convened relevant departments to discuss it. The review opinions indicate that the threshold for collecting inheritance tax will be raised from 3,000 yuan to 5,000 yuan. This is because families with assets below 5,000 yuan in China are only marginally better off than the extremely poor. Therefore, raising the collection threshold to 5,000 yuan is intended to consider the needs of the less affluent. At the same time, the progressive tax rates stipulated in the original draft have been slightly modified. The implementation period is not necessarily after the income tax is levied. (Central News Agency Telegram, 21st)

The Importance and Promotion of Literacy Campaigns (Middle) 90

Section Chief of the Ministry of Education, Zhong Lingxiu

3. Several Methods to Improve the Promotion of Literacy Campaigns in the Future

There are 300 million illiterate people in our country who should receive literacy education. Of these, over 6.79 million people have already become literate through public schools, accounting for only 2.7% of the illiterate population. More than 97% of those who should receive literacy education have not yet received it. Therefore, we feel that literacy campaigns should be actively promoted. Moreover, from the 17th to the 23rd year of the Republic, a total of only over 6.7 million people became literate over seven years, an average of just over one million people receiving literacy education per year. If this method continues, it will take 100 years to eliminate illiteracy among the 300 million illiterate people. This is a serious and urgent problem. Therefore, the methods for promoting literacy campaigns in the future must be improved. However, this matter is important and deserves careful research and discussion. I hope that my compatriots, especially those in the education sector, will conduct more research and discussion in order to obtain the most effective, economical, and thorough solution for the government to use. I will now present a few personal opinions for everyone to discuss:

In my personal opinion, there are only two steps to popularizing literacy education: the first step is to hold literacy campaigns to widely publicize to illiterate people the pain of illiteracy and the importance of literacy; the second step is to open more literacy places, such as public schools and literacy schools, so that the general public has places and opportunities to become literate and read. However, in addition to public schools and literacy schools with fixed schedules and courses, more mobile literacy places should be established, such as literacy stations, question-asking stations, open-air schools, mobile teaching, lantern slide education, door-to-door teaching, or using methods such as the "little teacher" system and family students, with the determination to "welcome those who come and deliver to those who do not," so that illiterate people who have difficulties in life and lack time can get opportunities to become literate and read anytime and anywhere. In addition, compulsory education should also be actively promoted in parallel. Because the current young and adult illiterates are all left over from the lack of compulsory education in the past, so there are as many as 300 million illiterates in the country. If compulsory education in our country had been popularized earlier, as in European and American countries, there would definitely not be so many illiterates now. Therefore, popularizing compulsory education is a fundamental solution to eliminating illiteracy. Otherwise, the number of illiterates will continue to increase day by day, and literacy campaigns will never end. Fortunately, the current government is able to equally value the popularization of compulsory education and the popularization of public education, a fundamental solution that addresses the symptoms and causes.

To achieve the goal of universal literacy, it is necessary to implement compulsion, with the government making the greatest determination to strictly supervise and promote it within a limited time. The method can be to first compel illiterate people between the ages of 16 and 30 as the first phase. After the first phase is completed, people between the ages of 30 and 40 will be compelled as the second phase. After the second phase is completed, people between the ages of 40 and 50 will be compelled as the third phase. This phased approach will be more economical in terms of manpower and financial resources.

The promotion of literacy education should have a dedicated responsible agency to be strictly enforced, as well as perform investigations and assessments. This agency should work closely with local administrative agencies, autonomous agencies, and military and police agencies to discuss progress. The Ministry of Education will issue key points for the organization of public education committees in counties and cities, which can be used for reference in establishing public education committees to carry out and plan all aspects of literacy education in coordination.

Illiterate people have the obligation to receive literacy education, and literate people have the obligation to teach illiterate people to read. This obligation cannot be exempted under any circumstances. In recent years, various localities have organized labor service groups, and it is most appropriate for literate people to undertake this kind of labor, which can also save a lot of teacher expenses. I hope that literate compatriots will work hard to serve the country and society, and to seek happiness for the people. This is everyone's inescapable duty and a heavenly duty that everyone should be happy to undertake.

The criteria for illiteracy are defined as those who cannot write their own name, age, place of origin, address, and occupation, cannot read simple books and newspapers, and cannot write simple ordinary letters. They are the targets for the implementation of literacy education. We should conduct clear area surveys so that they can receive literacy education.

In addition to the three types of Sanmin Zhuyi Thousand Character Primers A, B, and C compiled by the Ministry of Education and the literacy textbooks published by the Educational Book Bureau, surveys should be conducted on the characters needed by people in various localities and occupations, and various vocabularies and literacy common sense textbooks should be edited as supplementary reading materials. The teaching materials should pay attention to the following aspects: (1) They must meet the needs of the people's lives. (2) They must meet the psychological needs of the people. (3) They must be close to the people's experiences. (4) They must be able to express the people's aesthetic sense. (5) They must be able to cultivate the people's personality. (6) They must be in line with civic education.

Educational administrative agencies should encourage various bookstores to edit more various simple reading materials and sell them at low prices so that literate people can read more and continue to become literate, review, and further their studies.

Those who are illiterate and teach others to read after becoming literate should be rewarded according to the number of people they have taught and their achievements.

For those who have graduated from public schools and are literate, regulations should be made for continuing to review and practice using the characters they have learned, such as writing letters, reading newspapers, keeping accounts, writing diaries, and reading public supplementary reading materials and simple stories and novels. The original teachers should provide guidance, or other designated personnel should be assigned to allow literate people to have opportunities and convenience for continuing to review and further their studies.

The most difficult problems in actively promoting literacy education are generally said to be the three items of school buildings, teachers, and funding. However, our China is a poor country and should come up with poor methods to bury ourselves in hard work in order to achieve the goal of eliminating illiteracy. For example, regarding the issue of school buildings, we do not need magnificent school buildings. We only need to borrow existing houses from various schools, groups, public agencies, ancestral halls, guild halls, temples, etc. for use as school buildings without having to raise funds to build school buildings. Regarding teachers, we have one-quarter of literate compatriots, 100 million people, and 300 million illiterate people. If a literate person can be responsible for teaching three illiterate people to read, this major problem of eliminating illiteracy can be solved.

Page 9

Japanese Survey of Cultivated Land in the Puppet Binjiang Province 91

Fertile Land Deemed Ideal Agricultural Immigration Area

7.26 Million Hectares of Cultivated Land in 27 Counties

Harbin Correspondence: The northeastern three provinces and the South Manchuria area are relatively densely populated, so their land has long been developed. The North Manchuria area has fertile land that is no less than South Manchuria, but its population is not as prolific as South Manchuria. The Japanese deem it an ideal agricultural immigration area. Their initial plan is to conduct surveys and statistics. The Japanese first surveyed the 27 counties under the jurisdiction of the puppet Binjiang Province, the most fertile area in North Manchuria, and found that the cultivated area reached 7.26 million hectares. It is reported that the cultivated area in the previous year was only 1.15 million hectares. In the past, the landlords in various counties were squeezed by Japanese puppet corrupt officials and heavy taxes, and the land prices were very low, so they abandoned the land. In addition, there was a lot of uncultivated land due to water damage and unstable security. Currently, the Manchurian-Russian border is tense, and Japanese troops are gathered in North Manchuria. Developing agricultural areas has the intention of stationing troops, and security groups are organized to engage in defense. According to Japanese statistics, the cultivated area this year has greatly increased. The following is a list of arable land and cultivated land in 27 counties of the puppet Binjiang Province (unit: hectare):

De Wang's Representative Bao Yueqing Returns to Beiping from Bailingmiao 92

De Wang Sends Ao Yuzhang to Visit Fu Zuoyi

Bao Talks About De Wang's Support for the Central Government, Without Carrying Disloyalty Beiping Correspondence: Bao Yueqing, representative of the Mongolian Political Council of Bailingmiao stationed in Beiping, left Beiping for Pangjiang before the Mongolian rumors were rampant to visit Demchugdongrub, Vice Chairman of the Council, for consultation. Since then, he has traveled between the Miao and the River, and the news of his return to Beiping has been silent. During this period, the six counties of Chahar North were occupied by the puppet army of Li Shouxin, who advanced from Duolun and advocated a false title, causing the attitude of De Wang to be more widely rumored, and it was said that he had joined the puppet army in Chahar North. As a result of the rumors, the general public had unlimited disappointment in the Mongolian Political Council of Bailingmiao.

After the establishment of the Mongolian Political Council in Suiyuan, De Wang's attitude has been even more noteworthy. Yun Jixian, Director of the Security Office of the Mongolian Political Council of Bailingmiao, led his troops to withdraw. When the telegram came, all parties suspected that the Council had announced its dissolution. Until recently, De Wang seemed to have made a factual clarification due to the fear of people's words. First, he sent a representative, Ao Yuzhang, from Bailingmiao to Sui to visit Fu Zuoyi, Chairman of Suiyuan. Then, he ordered his representative in Beiping, Bao Yueqing, to go from Pangjiang through Chahar North to Zhangjiakou to visit Zhang Zizhong, Chairman of Chahar, and made the same statement. Bao then arrived in Beiping at 7:00 AM this (20th) morning.

After Bao arrived in Beiping, visitors came in an endless stream, including two Japanese, whose names are unknown. It is said that they were paying a visit. Bao visited Song Zheyuan, Chairman of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council, at Wuyiku at 10:00 AM that morning and made a sincere statement on behalf of De Wang. They talked for an hour before he left. According to side news about the content of the Song-Bao conversation, Song was extremely concerned about the severe snow disaster in Mongolia and promised to find ways to solicit donations for emergency relief. Bao made a thorough analysis of De Wang's attitude and believed that the various rumors outside were not credible. He asked Song to report to the Central Government on his behalf. Song expressed his admiration for De Wang's loyalty and patriotism. Therefore, the result of the conversation was extremely satisfactory. The reporter went to Bao's residence for an interview at noon. Bao answered each of the questions: "The Mongolian Political Council of Suiyuan was established when Mongolian rumors were rampant. Although it caused a lot of suspicion among the general public, in fact, the Council is one of the subordinate agencies of the Bailingmiao Mongolian Council, which is not surprising. In the near future, the Alxa Banner will also have the same agency. This is purely for the convenience of handling autonomy, and it is by no means Mongolian separation. Therefore, De Wang's attitude can be summed up in one sentence: "Supporting the Central Government, without carrying disloyalty." The opposition between the Miao and Sui Councils has been self-evident. Until now, the Suiyuan Mongolian Council has sent a special commissioner to be stationed in the Temple River on a regular basis, and the Temple River Mongolian Council has also set up an office in Suiyuan, responsible by Ao Yunzhang." Bao continued, "Since De Wang's attitude is clear, the external rumors have been self-defeating. As far as he knows, the puppet army government in Chahar North, instigated by Zhuo Shihuai and Li Shouxin, has not been established. Zhuo Shihuai is now in the cattle and sheep flocks, and Li is staying in Zhangbei County. The number of people in the two departments has not increased. The recent situation in the six counties is also peaceful. It is completely unfounded to say that Li's troops were stationed in Bailingmiao. Because the training group under De Wang's jurisdiction recently changed into yellow clothing, this caused this misunderstanding. As for Yun Jixian, the Director of the Security Office of the Temple River Mongolian Council, who defected, he is now stationed in Saxian. De Wang decided to order the guns and ammunition carried away by his troops to be returned to the Temple River Mongolian Council. Ao Yuzhang is now contacting Chairman Fu in Suiyuan to hand over the guns and ammunition. It will be resolved satisfactorily soon. Wu Heling, a member of the Mongolian Tibetan Council, also felt that the journey was dangerous because Ni Guanzhou was killed in Zhangbei, so he stayed in Pangjiang to assist De Wang in handling foreign affairs. The rumors that he was also killed are not true. Wu has already scheduled to come to Beiping within a month and transfer back to Nanjing." Finally, the reporter asked Bao about the tragic snow disaster in Mongolia. He said, "In previous years, Mongolian winter snowfalls were around 100 days. Unexpectedly, after the snowfall started in October last year, it has not cleared up until now. The snow on the plains is between four and five feet deep, and the low-lying areas are even deeper. Because the grass source has been cut off, cattle and sheep first eat each other's hair, and then they wither and starve to death. The number is 99 percent. Wealthy households with 3,000 heads of cattle and sheep have become impoverished. At the same time, a fuel panic has occurred. Since there is no more livestock dung, the Mongolian yurts are dismantled for fuel. The tragic situation is no less than a river flood. Therefore, De Wang first established a fundraising association in Pangjiang and ordered his subordinates to report the details of the losses in order to raise funds for relief as a whole. In the near future, De Wang will send a special commissioner to Beijing to appeal for relief. I am entering Beijing to wait for the telegram order, but it is believable that I will not go elsewhere in the short term in order to contact the local authorities here at any time."

According to Mongolian sources, the Japanese Kwantung Army now has a special agency in Bailingmiao. The head of the agency is named Quanhai, who travels back and forth between Bailingmiao and Pangjiang. Japanese aircraft are also constantly found in Pangjiang. As for the number of puppet troops in Chahar North, Li and Zhuo have a total of more than 3,000 people. Their number is called the Chahar East Army. The people in the six counties are groaning and complaining because they cannot bear the supply and disturbance. If this continues, it is feared that it will trigger a civil unrest. (20th)

The Hebei Authorities to Conduct a Thorough Elimination of Communist Bandits in Southern Hebei 93

Four Counties Including Yaoshan Designated as an Administrative Region

At the Same Time, Suppression of the Poor People's Society in Western Hebei

Baoding Dispatch: Since the Communist bandits disturbed Shanxi, Hebei Chairman Song Zheyuan, considering the close proximity and relations between Hebei and Shanxi provinces, and the extreme importance of border defense, has not only deployed strong defenses in key fortresses, but also sent Security Director Zhang Yunrong to various counties in western and southern Hebei to supervise the stationed troops and local militias, strictly preventing banditry. However, in the Yaoshan, Julu, and Renxian areas of southern Hebei, Communist bandits still lie hidden. In the Pingshan, Lingshou, and Jingxing areas of western Hebei, there is an illegal organization called the Poor People's Society. After deliberation on countermeasures, it was decided to use political power to promote their awakening and self-renewal. Furthermore, Yaoshan, Renxian, Julu, and Neiqiu counties will be unified into one district, with a special administrative commissioner appointed to be responsible for all bandit suppression and pacification matters within the territory. Su Shen Zhang Jinchen was appointed as the magistrate of Yaoshan County and concurrently the administrative commissioner of the Yaoshan District. Zhang was one of the pioneers in this province to advocate the establishment of a defense corps to promote people's self-defense, and he formerly served as the president of Hebei University, having a good understanding of politics. After the establishment of the Tanggu Truce, Zhang was ordered to enter the war zone to manage a certain county, achieving considerable success. Afterwards, he used his personal savings to establish a defense corps, personally going to various counties for leadership. This time, the provincial government entrusted him with full responsibility for the four counties. He undoubtedly has policies to resolve the Communist bandits within the territory. Furthermore, the provincial government holds the utmost determination to thoroughly eliminate the Communist bandits lurking in the localities. Therefore, the militias of the four counties in the Yaoshan District are completely placed under Zhang's command. Song Zheyuan also ordered Liu Zhensan's troops to be stationed within the territory of the district to assist Zhang in eliminating the Communist bandits. Therefore, the banditry in southern Hebei can gradually be resolved and eliminated.

The Pingshan, Lingshou, and Jingxing areas of western Hebei are located in a border region, situated at the foot of the Taihang Mountains. The territory is crisscrossed by mountains, and transportation is extremely inconvenient, resulting in it becoming a haven for petty criminals. Furthermore, due to the economic bankruptcy of the rural areas in recent years and the difficulties in the lives of the farmers, the farmers with weak wills are extremely susceptible to the instigation of villains. Since the summer, illegal organizations of the Poor People's Society have emerged in various places. The leaders of the society are mostly intellectuals, raising the deceptive banner of "distributing grain" and "equalizing wealth," propagating everywhere, and inciting the masses. They also used gangsters from the city to act recklessly. By winter, their power had grown stronger, and the number of people joining had gradually increased, many of whom were local ruffians and vagrants lacking clothing and food. They often summoned gatherings to rob villages, and they posted slogans with absurd language everywhere in densely populated areas such as market towns and temple fairs. As a result, people's hearts were unsettled. Although the local authorities repeatedly wanted to suppress them, they ultimately felt powerless due to the long distances and inconvenient transportation. Moreover, many of the bandits were villagers without obvious markings, and the leaders among them were even more secretive and difficult to find. The common people also harbored suspicions of each other, and even if they suffered minor losses, they did not dare to report to the authorities for fear of causing greater trouble. This caused the banditry to become increasingly rampant, and the local wealthy households were repeatedly robbed. The bandits killed and set fires without any scruples. In Mupan Village in Pingshan County, bandits were entrenched, numbering as many as seven or eight hundred people. The local militia police were ordered to search and suppress them many times, but it was difficult to completely eliminate them. At this moment, the Security Bureau is supervising Pingshan County and neighboring counties to jointly defend and suppress them. (20th)

Agricultural Guidance Committees Established in Various Counties of Guangdong Province 94

—Afforestation to be Expanded This Year—

Guangzhou Dispatch: In recent years, the counties of Guangdong Province have spared no effort in promoting agricultural and forestry undertakings. Special attention has been paid to afforestation, which has been included in the three-year administrative plan and circulated for strict implementation. Many of the barren hills in various places have been developed into forest farms in a timely manner, guiding the people to promote afforestation in order to increase farmers' production and develop the rural economy. Plans for expanding the promotion of afforestation and holding afforestation movement publicity weeks have been developed and implemented by various counties. The Agricultural and Forestry Extension Office has widely purchased tree seedlings and distributed them to farmers for planting, so that the barren land in various counties can be established as forestry areas to implement afforestation plans. The model forest farm in the Eastern District has also increased the purchase of tree seedlings for the purpose of implementing an expanded afforestation movement, and has issued notices to various county districts and villages for planting. This method is undoubtedly beneficial to the promotion of the afforestation plan. Furthermore, counties that have not yet established forest farms are now planning to complete them within this year, and have also decided to establish rice seed propagation farms and district and township nurseries, vigorously expanding forestry and improving agricultural products, so that farmers' lives can be effectively assisted. In addition, regarding the research and improvement of agricultural methods, it is planned that each county will establish a guidance committee, assigning personnel with rich agricultural knowledge and experience to engage in guiding rural improvement, paying attention to the development of crops in order to universalize and improve them.

Travel Notes from Hunan and Guangdong (10) (Travel Correspondence from Our Newspaper Reporter) Feelings After Returning 95

The entire Guangdong-Hankou Railway has been connected, and the date is already imminent. This is something that all Chinese people unanimously believe is joyful. However, according to my observations, the entire line being connected is something to be celebrated, but it seems that there are still difficulties in the full operation of the entire line. This is something that the authorities must pay close attention to. First, the Guangdong-Hankou Railway is currently divided into three sections. The sleepers of the Hunan-Hubei section are rotten, and the train moves as bumpily as a cradle, as I have mentioned before. The southern section is in better condition, but the vehicles are extremely old and unclean. Only the Zhuzhou-Shaoguan section, being a newly built line, is in excellent condition. It is like a body where the head and feet are sick, but the abdomen is healthy. What good is a healthy abdomen if the head and feet are sick? Therefore, the most important task in the future is to find ways to treat the head and feet, striving to make them as healthy as the abdomen, so that the whole body can develop evenly. I have heard that the Ministry of Railways has established a reorganization committee, which is intended to seek the soundness of the entire Guangdong-Hankou line. I wonder if there are concrete plans in terms of funding? Second, the Zhuzhou-Shaoguan section ordered a large number of 4-8-4 type giant locomotives from the United Kingdom, capable of traveling 40 kilometers per hour, but only a few have been delivered, and they will not all arrive until November of this year. These giant locomotives do not seem to be able to handle the railway tracks of the Hunan-Hubei section and the southern section. Before the head and feet are healthy, if these locomotives are used to travel the entire line, it will inevitably lead to head injuries and broken feet, which would be unwise. In my opinion, before the Hunan-Hubei section and the southern section have been completely reorganized, train operations should still be divided into three sections: from Wuchang Xujiapeng to Changsha, from Changsha to Lechang, and from Lechang to Guangzhou. In this way, there will be no bias towards the heavy and the light. If the train schedule is properly arranged, there will be no inconvenience for passengers. Third, the reason why the road administration of the Hunan-Hubei section and the southern section are not maintained is that the income is exhausted and there is no money for cultivation. However, since it is not possible to increase revenue, there is only one way to reduce expenditure. When the Ministry of Railways decides to reorganize the road affairs of the two sections, it should study how to improve the business of the two sections. How can revenue be increased, or how can expenditure be reduced? A fundamental solution should be obtained. Otherwise, even if huge sums of money are allocated for large-scale reorganization, it can only be gratifying for a while, and it is not possible to expect it to last for a long time.

The above is a humble opinion on the overall reorganization of the entire line. There are also other aspects, such as promoting scenic spots and promoting freight transport, which I will also present, even if I am ignorant: First, promoting scenic spots. The Guangdong-Hankou Railway passes through the three provinces of Hubei, Hunan, and Guangdong, with a total length of 1,096 kilometers. The cities along the line, such as Guangzhou, Shaozhou, Hengyang, Changsha, Yuezhou, and Wuchang, are all large cities, and their famous scenic spots and historical sites are well known to the world and do not need to be repeated. The smaller cities, with their waterfront villages shrouded in mist, green waters, and verdant mountains, are also extremely expansive and magnificent, but unfortunately, their fame has not been established and cannot be revealed. To list what I know: In Guangdong Province, there are the Fulu Shou Mountains in Lechang, the Taihe Cave in Yinzhanjun, and the Feilai Temple, Cangxia Cave, and Feixia Cave in Pajiangkou. The Blind Man's Gorge, Yangying Gorge, Stone General Temple, and Cao Zhu Niangniang Temple in Lianjiangkou. The Lengcang Rock, Zhupo Rock, Li Fan Stele, and Nanshan Temple in Yingde. The Cuihua Pavilion, Shunfeng Temple, Furong Mountain, Nanhua Temple, and Jiucheng Terrace in Shaozhou. The Han Wengong Temple, Xishi Rock, Meishan Waterfall, and Jiulong Shibatan in Lechang. The Jinji Ridge in Pingshi. In Hunan Province, there are the Mengyan and Genyan in Yizhang. The Su Xian Ridge, Yidi Tomb, Chayu Pavilion, and hot spring baths in Chenzhou. The Fengchu Pavilion, Cai Zi Pond, Du Fu Tomb, and Ma Fu Ridge in Leiyang. The Three Gian Daifu Tomb in Miluo, etc. All of the above have considerable historical value and are worthy of sightseeing. In my opinion, it seems appropriate to work with local people to find ways to promote the scenic spots and historical sites along the railway line: repair and organize them properly. For those that are farther away, roads can also be built to make them more convenient. Attracting tourists is the way to benefit the local area, and it is also the way to increase railway revenue. Second, promoting freight transport. The products along the Guangdong-Hankou Railway, such as Guangdong's industrial textiles, salt and seafood, aquatic vegetables, coal, tobacco, tea, wood, etc., Hunan's Hunan embroidery, soybeans, ramie, pigs, rice, umbrellas, tung oil, etc., and Hubei's tea bricks, charcoal, rice, etc., are too numerous to mention, and Hunan's products are the most abundant. Regarding railway freight, since the Ministry of Railways implemented responsible transport, it has strived for commercialization, eliminating the previous malpractices, and the business of each line has been revitalized. However, what I mean by promoting freight transport is how to help merchants develop their business and promote freight transport. The products of Hunan and Guangdong are so abundant, but the old-fashioned merchants may not be able to pay much attention to the supply and demand of goods and the method of packaging. The railway should show them the financial situation in various places, the level of living, the purchasing power of society, and general preferences. At the same time, in terms of packaging, it should also plan with the simplest, strongest, most economical, and most convenient methods. In this way, the railway and the merchants become one, depending on each other like lips and teeth. When the business of the merchants is developed, the promotion of railway freight will also achieve twice the result with half the effort.

In addition, everything I witnessed in the places I passed through, whether general social matters or aspects of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway, was very vigorous, with no signs of inertia, which is truly gratifying. However, on the way back, I visited Macau, where everything I saw was evil. Smoking and gambling are everywhere. Since the governing authorities levy taxes on this, there is no value in criticism. However, from Macau to Zhongshan, the Qiguan Highway is as smooth as an arrow, with clear streams and ancient trees, and the scenery is beautiful, which makes travelers appreciate it. (The End)

Kunshan to Enlarge the Celebration of Children's Day

The April 4th Children's Day will arrive in an instant. All circles in Wei County are preparing to enlarge the celebration. The three agencies of the County Party Department, the County Government, and the Education Bureau have been designated to be responsible for the implementation, and the method has been decided. Notify all agencies, groups, and shops to fly flags for celebration. At 9:00 AM, a celebration ceremony will be held at the stadium. A lantern parade will be held in the evening, gathering at the stadium at 5:30 PM for departure. Each household should prepare lanterns and candles, and all agencies and people are welcome to participate. At 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the same day, three outstanding students from each school in the urban area will be selected as representatives to gather on time, form a team to the county government, and pay respects to the officials. A letter was sent to the Chamber of Commerce notifying stores selling children's items to offer special discounts on that day. A health education exhibition will be held, hosted by the Education Bureau.

Reconstruction of Two Ancient Sites Completed

The Ma'anshan Mountain in the north of this county has pleasant scenery and is frequented by tourists. The ancient Ming Dynasty sites of Wenbi Peak and Yufeng Pavilion on the top of the mountain have been in disrepair for many years and are in ruins. Last spring, County Magistrate Peng Baichuan initiated fundraising for reconstruction, which has now been completed, costing more than 3,000 yuan. A stone monument has also been erected to leave a lasting impression.

Japanese Officers Arrive in Suzhou One After Another

Twenty Japanese officers arrived in Suzhou yesterday morning from Shanghai in four special cars along the Shanghai-Suzhou Highway. The county government, upon receiving a notification from the Shanghai Municipal Government and the provincial government, immediately instructed the Public Security Bureau to provide protection. The acting director, Yan Jishi, immediately dispatched the Flying Team Inspector Qiang Zhang Jiahu to lead the police in cars to Kunshan to welcome them. They then accompanied the officers on a week-long inspection of the Suzhou-Jiashan Highway at places such as Shidai Bridge outside the city. At 1:00 PM in the afternoon, they left Suzhou and went in the direction of the Suzhou-Changzhou Highway. Inspector Qiang and others followed in cars for protection. At around 2:00 PM in the afternoon, the Public Security Bureau received another report that another eighteen Japanese officers had arrived in Suzhou.

The Stonecutter Strike Resolved

More than four hundred quarry workers at Jiaoshan Quarry, Shimatou, Mudu Township, went on strike to demand a wage increase from the mine owners, but failed. It is now known that after the Mudu Township Chief Wang Shujie worked hard to mediate between the representatives of both labor and management, the wages were increased by one-fourth, which satisfied both parties. All the workers resumed work as usual yesterday (21st). Chief Wang came to Suzhou on the 21st to pay respects to County Magistrate Deng and report on the course of the strike.

Rice Prices Soar, Crackdown on Hoarding

The price of rice in Suzhou has been rising continuously for ten days. Although it has recently fallen slightly, there are still signs of continued rises. In total, it has risen by 1.2 yuan within ten days, and the general public is crying out in agony. According to a report from the General Labor Union to the County Party Department, this soaring rice price must be due to unscrupulous merchants hoarding and speculating, monopolizing the market price. They requested strict crackdowns and efforts to suppress rice prices. Special Commissioner Sun specially ordered the County Chamber of Commerce to convene a meeting of rice industry representatives for reply. The County Chamber of Commerce replied to the County Party Department yesterday (21st), saying that due to various reasons, the inventory of rice shops in Suzhou is limited. If they are not purchased in the spring, there will inevitably be panic when the harvest is not yet available in late spring or early summer. This is not hoarding and speculation. As for the rice price issue, it should be requested that the County Party Department work with the County Government to find a solution.

Wuxi Strictly Prohibits Unscrupulous Merchants from Manipulating Copper Coins

The Tongye Gonghui (guild) of twenty-one industries in Mu County, including the wine, soy sauce, and tobacco industries, recently reported that the exchange rate of copper coins in Wuxi is unstable. They specially requested the provincial and county authorities to find a way to stop it "and requested that it be handled in accordance with the methods stipulated by the ministry." County Magistrate Long, after receiving the report, stated that the exchange rate of legal tender in this county was determined by the former county magistrate in November of last year after inviting industry and commerce groups for discussion. It was temporarily standardized at 300 copper coins worth ten each per yuan, with the highest not exceeding 310 coins and the lowest not less than 290 coins. Recently, the exchange rate of legal tender on the market has risen to more than 310 coins per yuan, which is obviously being manipulated by someone for other purposes. This is indeed inappropriate. Yesterday, a public notice was issued strictly prohibiting unauthorized changes to the exchange rate of legal tender and arbitrary rises and falls thereafter. Anyone who dares to deliberately violate the prohibition will be severely punished without any leniency.

Zhenjiang Provincial Party Department Officials Appointed

Since taking office after being sworn in, the Special Commissioner of the Provincial Party Department has been actively planning the future work promotion plan of Jiangsu Provincial Party Affairs and the internal adjustment methods of the Party Department. The First Special Commissioner Meeting was held on the 20th, and it was resolved that the offices in various districts would be abolished, with a deadline for completion within this month. Old staff members will be re-employed, including Chen Tao, Chief of the Organization Section, Zhou Huapeng, Chief of the Propaganda Section, Shi Shunyuan, Chief of the Mass Training Section, Liu Chengrui, Chief of the General Affairs Section, Zhang Xiaoyou (Director), Wang Zhenxian (Deputy Director), Zhang Guanqiu, Zhu Lujiu, Liu Rentao, Ji Zhanbei, Zhang Jinchun, Su Bao President Chen Kanghe, Su Bao Manager Zeng Binggan, and Xu Bao President Duan Muzhen. Bian Zongmeng was recommended as the standing director of the Provincial New Life Movement Promotion Association.

Jiaxing The Second Phase of Baozhang (Neighborhood Head) Training Scheduled

The Baozhang training held by the county government, the first phase of which is scheduled to be completed at the end of this month. Following this, the second phase of Baozhang training will be held. The county government has ordered all township and town offices to ensure that all Baozhang who have not yet received training will be trained in the second phase. Regulations have been set, and anyone who is deemed incapable of receiving training will be dismissed and replaced. Each township and town is ordered to screen and report the names for verification by March 25.

Changshu The Embezzlement of Education Funds Case Concluded

The case of Hua Zhaozeng, the former accountant of the Education Bureau, embezzling funds amounting to more than 75,000 yuan a few years ago, caused a sensation at the time, and is now completely closed with 952 yuan returned. The case originated in 1933, when the accounting office of the Education Bureau discovered that Hua Zhaozeng, the accountant of the rent collection office, had embezzled funds. After detailed investigation, the amount was shockingly high, reaching more than 75,000 yuan. Hua was sent to the county for investigation and handling. At that time, the education sector was extremely shocked. Hua voluntarily offered to compensate for the embezzlement and was released on bail by ten money shops. Hua disappeared without a trace like a yellow crane. The county government sentenced the guarantor Gao Zilin to one year in prison, but the embezzled funds could not be recovered. It was later discovered that Hua was a native of Wuxi and had some land in Wuxi. The county sent a letter to the Wuxi County government requesting that his land be auctioned off. It was not until the beginning of this month that someone agreed to buy the property for 952 yuan. The Education Bureau of this county went to Wuxi to collect the money, and thus this major embezzlement case of education funds was concluded with a compensation of one-thousandth and five percent.

Fire in the Park

All the houses in the North Gate Park have been built by individuals and teahouses have been opened. Among them, there is the Huan Cui Xia Zhu, which is the most magnificent place in the entire park. Its tea customers are mostly local so-called gentry, retired administrative personnel, and current government employees who lead affluent and leisurely lives. Therefore, although it is nominally called a teahouse, it is actually a club for people who hold county political power, and outsiders rarely set foot in it. As a result, society calls it the Huan Cui faction. The designated regular tea customers of this place rarely miss the morning and evening sessions. Unexpectedly, at about 9:30 PM on the 19th, a fire suddenly broke out in the kitchen behind the Huan Cui Xia Zhu, and the flames instantly burst through the roof. Fortunately, the teahouse staff quickly reported to the Fire Brigade and went to extinguish the fire. The teahouse in front was not affected, and only the doors and windows were destroyed. Alas, the Huan Cui faction is about to lose its residence.

Nantong Coastal Fishing Season in Northern Jiangsu

Along the coast of northern Jiangsu, squid are arriving, and the yellow croaker are about to arrive. Representatives of the fishing associations of Nantong, Rugao, Haimen, Dongtai, Yancheng, and Qidong counties met in Nantong on the 20th to discuss important cases of self-defense during the fishing season. The three major brigades of the Provincial Marine Police have all been stationed along the coast and equipped with patrol boats to protect fishermen at sea.

Nantong will hold labor services from the 28th of this month to the 1st of April to build the ring road. All fields and houses encroaching on the city foundation must be demolished by the stipulated date. The road construction project will be inaugurated by the Special Commissioner. Jiashan Seven Lives Lost in a Terrible Fire

The Jiang Temple in the Xiluo Wanbang of Yangmiao Town worships the idol of Wen Da Tianjun, and its incense has always been said to be very prosperous. The 19th of this month was the date of Tianjun's temple fair. On this day, a night fair was held as usual, and all the young men and women from various villages participated in the grand event. Only the elderly and children were left to guard the homes. Unexpectedly, at around 11:00 PM, a fire suddenly broke out in a certain house, and the red flames soared into the sky. The wind was strong, and when the farmers learned of the fire and rushed back to rescue it, all 14 tile houses in the village had been burned down. Shen Meilai's mother, 76 years old, Shen Fuxing's mother, Mrs. Zhang, 68 years old, and Shen Yinkui's daughter, 13 years old, and Shen Heshang's son, 9 years old, and Shen Deguan's son, not older than 7 years, were burned to death. Their heads, hands, and feet were burned, and their entire bodies were charred beyond recognition. The scene was horrifying, and the cries shook the heavens. The losses amounted to more than several thousand gold.

Ningbo Huang Shaohong Visits Ningbo

Hangzhou The Yuyao Salt Dispute Resurfaces

The Yuyao salt dispute was mediated by the Shaoxing Administrative Inspector's Office, and three resolutions were agreed upon: salt merchants would advance 65,000 yuan, and the collection of salt would be resumed at 40% starting from the 20th. The dispute could have been resolved, but in order to break the bad habits of Pengchang's handling of exploitation of salt farmers, the Salt Transport Department sent a weighman from the salt field to the warehouse to carry out the weighing. More than 100 people in Yuyao field, seeing that their own interests were being harmed, incited carters to strike, causing salt to be unable to be transported to the warehouse, and the collection of salt was suspended again. The field director and the storage merchants have separately telegraphed the Liangjiang Salt Transport Department for instructions, and tax police will be sent to forcefully stop it, and Pengchang, the leader, will be arrested. The dispute can then be resolved, and the livelihood of the salt farmers can be maintained.

Huili Bank Suspends Business for Liquidation

Hangzhou Huili Bank, which opened in Qinghefang Lane Xinyu Lane, has been around for more than ten years. The manager was the late Wang Zhuqi, a well-known figure in the Hangzhou business community. After Wang's death, the deputy manager Shu Shen'an was promoted to manager. However, the bank's capital was less than 150,000 yuan, and the scope of business could not be greatly expanded. In recent years, due to the impact of the economic downturn, the bank had a large number of bad debts from shops, making it difficult to meet depositors' withdrawals. A temporary shareholders meeting was held on the afternoon of the 19th. Due to the difficulty of increasing shares, it was decided to suspend business and entrust lawyer Chen Huimin to liquidate. The bank's debts and receivables can be offset against each other, and there is no impact on the financial market.

Port A Counterfeit Coin Trafficking Ring Busted

Kuang Liandeng, a local resident living in Yuqing Lane in District 1, made a living by secretly trafficking in counterfeit subsidiary coins. Each time, his wife, Kuang Zhang, and a woman named Zheng Wen, specialized in trafficking from Shanghai to Bengbu, and no one recognized them. The counterfeit subsidiary coins they transported were mostly two-corner banknotes. Every 100 yuan of counterfeit banknotes could be sold for 45 yuan of legal tender. Their secret sales agency was set up in Kuang's home. Recently, a Lu man named Wang Cunde went to traffic them and was noticed by the gang police in District 1, who reported it to the bureau for arrest. Sixty-nine counterfeit two-corner banknotes were found on the two women, Kuang and Zheng, who were arrested along with Wang Cunde and sent to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. The main culprit, Kuang Liandeng, escaped without a trace. On the 19th, the three male and female criminals were transferred to the local court to be tried for crimes of obstructing monetary credit.

The Central Bank Will Send Personnel to the Countryside to Exchange Legal Tender 105

Expenses Will Be Subsidized by the Ministry

Approved by the Ministry of Finance

According to the Times News Agency, although the method of exchanging legal tender has been extended to May 3rd, there is still a large number of silver coins hidden among the people in our vast country's remote provinces that have not been exchanged for legal tender. Now, in order to facilitate the people's exchange and to avoid the people being misunderstood and detained by the military and police for carrying cash on their own to exchange for legal tender, the Central Bank has specially consulted and approved the Ministry of Finance to order all its branches throughout the country to send personnel carrying legal tender to villages and places where there are no agencies for exchanging legal tender to exchange silver coins for legal tender among the people. As for the expenses required by the Central Bank for handling this exchange procedure, the Ministry of Finance has also agreed to subsidize, but at most it cannot exceed 3% of the total amount of silver received. According to the Nanjing branch's report, it is planned to entrust reputable banks or commercial firms in provinces, cities, and counties to collect cash and give a handling fee of no more than 3%. After learning about the situation, the bank has sent a letter to the Ministry of Finance asking for permission to do so, and other branches that make the same request can also be handled in the same way. It is heard that the Ministry of Finance, after learning about the situation, will approve it in order to collect cash.

Tomorrow is the Anniversary of Deng Keng's Martyrdom 106

The Municipal Party Department Will Convene a Memorial Meeting

The Entire City Will Fly Flags at Half-Mast to Express Grief According to the Da Gong News Agency, tomorrow (March 23rd) is the 14th anniversary of the martyrdom of the late Mr. Deng Zhongyuan. The Central Standing Committee has decided to issue an order to the entire country to hold a memorial meeting on that day and fly flags at half-mast to express grief. After receiving the order, the Municipal Party Department decided to convene representatives from all walks of life at the party department's auditorium at 10 AM tomorrow to hold a memorial meeting. The details are recorded below:

History of Martyrdom The late Deng Zhongyuan, whose name was Keng, was from Huiyang, Guangdong. He followed Premier Sun Yat-sen to advocate revolution and was extremely loyal. Two years before the establishment of the Republic, during the Guangzhou New Army Uprising, he planned and launched the uprising with Zhao Boxian and others. On August 19th, one year before the establishment of the Republic, during the Wuchang Uprising, Mr. Deng Keng infiltrated Danshui and led the people's militia to launch an attack. Hu Hanmin served as the governor and Mr. Deng Keng served as the director of the Army Department and later as the garrison commander of Qiongyai. In the sixth year of the Republic, the military government was organized and he served as the chief of staff. When Premier Sun Yat-sen led the Northern Expedition, he relied on Deng's preparation of military pay and equipment. On March 20th of the eleventh year of the Republic, he went to Hong Kong due to an incident. He returned to the Guangdong capital the next day and was suddenly attacked by assassins just after leaving the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway Station, suffering two gunshot wounds. He died at 5 AM on the 23rd, at the age of only 38. Because the Central Government believed that Deng's achievements were great, the Standing Committee decided to designate that day as Deng's martyrdom anniversary.

Memorial Meeting The Municipal Party Department, after receiving the order, decided to convene representatives from all walks of life at the party department's auditorium in Fenglinqiao at 10 AM tomorrow to hold a memorial meeting. The order of the memorial is as follows: Opening of the meeting, singing the party song, bowing three times to the party flag, the national flag, and Premier Sun Yat-sen's portrait, reading Premier Sun Yat-sen's will, silent tribute for three minutes, chairman's report, speeches, shouting slogans, conclusion of the ceremony.

Flying Flags at Half-Mast All agencies, groups, schools, and party departments at all levels in the city, because tomorrow is the anniversary of the martyrdom of the late Mr. Deng Zhongyuan, designated by the Central Government, will all follow the order to fly flags at half-mast for one day to express their condolences.
